With c7=0: c5*epsilon*1. Then `T*c0*epsilon**3 + (c2+c5)*epsilon + c3 + c4*epsilon**2`. Missing T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 23:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2*epsilon + c3*epsilon + c4 + c5*epsilon**2 + c6*epsilon`
With c1=0, c2=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + (c3+c6)*epsilon + c4 + c5*epsilon**2`. Missing T and epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 24:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T**c2*c3 + c4*epsilon + c5 + c6*epsilon**2`
With c1=0, c2=1: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c3 + c4*epsilon + c5 + c6*epsilon**2`. Missing epsilon**3. Set c4=0, c6=0: still missing epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 25:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2 + T*c3/(T*c4+c5) + c6 + c7/(T*c4+c5) + c8*epsilon + c9*epsilon**2`
The rational terms in T make this non-polynomial in T. Setting c3=0, c7=0 eliminates them. With c1=0, c8=0, c9=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2 + c6`. Missing epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 26:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2 + c3 + c4*epsilon + c5*epsilon**2 + c6*log(T*c7+1)*|epsilon|**c8`
The log(T*c7+1) term is not polynomial in T. Setting c6=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2 + c3 + c4*epsilon + c5*epsilon**2`. Missing epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 27:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2 + c3 + c4*epsilon + c5*epsilon**2 + c6*(T+1)**c7`
With c7=1: c6*(T+1) = c6*T + c6. With c1=0, c4=0, c5=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2 + c3 + c6*T + c6` = `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*(c2+c6) + (c3+c6)`. Missing epsilon**3. 
With c7=0: c6*1. Same issue. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 28:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2 + T**c3*c4 + c5 + c6*epsilon + c7*epsilon**2`
With c1=0, c3=0 (T**0=1): `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2 + c4 + c5 + c6*epsilon + c7*epsilon**2`. Missing epsilon**3. Set c6=0, c7=0: still missing. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 29:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2 + c3*sin(T*c4+c5) + c6 + c7*epsilon + c8*epsilon**2`
sin term is not polynomial. Set c3=0. With c1=0, c7=0, c8=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2 + c6`. Missing epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 30:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2 + c3*epsilon + c4*epsilon**2`
With c1=0, c3=0, c4=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2`. Missing epsilon**3 and constant. Only 2 basis functions available (T*epsilon**3, T, epsilon, epsilon**2). Can't get epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 31:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + c2*epsilon + c3*exp(T*c4) + c5 + c6*epsilon**2`
exp(T*c4) is not polynomial. Set c4=0: c3*1. With c1=0, c2=0, c6=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c3 + c5`. Missing T and epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 32:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2 + c3*epsilon + c4 + c5*epsilon**2 + c6*epsilon`
With c1=0, c3=0, c5=0, c6=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2 + c4`. Missing epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 33:** Already analyzed. Missing epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 34:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2 + T*c3 + c4 + c5*epsilon + c6*epsilon**2`
Same as 33 essentially (T*c2 + T*c3 = T*(c2+c3)). Missing epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 35:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2 + c3*|epsilon| + c4 + c5*epsilon + c6*epsilon**2`
With epsilon≥0, |epsilon|=epsilon. With c1=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2 + (c3+c5)*epsilon + c4 + c6*epsilon**2`. Missing epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 36:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + c2*epsilon + c3*log(T*c4+1) + c5 + c6*epsilon**2`
log is not polynomial. Set c3=0. Missing T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 37:** Has exp and log terms. Setting c5=0 eliminates them. Then missing T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 38:** Has exp(sin(...)) term. Setting c5=0. Then missing T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 39:** Has log term. Setting c5=0. Then missing T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 40:** Has rational terms in T. Setting c2=0, c7=0 (or appropriate). With c1=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2/(T*c3+c4) + c5*epsilon + c6 + c7/(T*c3+c4) + c8*epsilon**2`. Rational terms can't match polynomial. Set c2=0, c7=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c5*epsilon + c6 + c8*epsilon**2`. Missing T and epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 41:** Has Max term. Setting c5=0. Then missing T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 42:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + c2 + c3*epsilon + c4*epsilon**2 + c5*epsilon`
With c1=0, c3=0, c4=0, c5=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c2`. Missing T and epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 43:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + c2*epsilon + c3 + c4*epsilon**2`
With c1=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c2*epsilon + c3 + c4*epsilon**2`. Missing T and epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 44:** Has sin term. Set c2=0. Then missing T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 45:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**c2 + c3*epsilon + c4 + c5*epsilon**2*exp(T*c6)`
With c1=0, c2=3: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c3*epsilon + c4 + c5*epsilon**2*exp(T*c6)`. The exp term is not polynomial. Set c5=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c3*epsilon + c4`. Missing T and epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 46:** `c0*epsilon + c1 + c2*(c3+|epsilon|)**4 + c4*exp(T*c5)*exp(c6*epsilon)`
Has epsilon**4 and exp terms. The (c3+|epsilon|)**4 with c3=0 gives epsilon**4. exp terms can't produce polynomial T dependence exactly. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 47:** Complex. Has 1/(c2+epsilon), epsilon**3, epsilon**c6, exp terms. Setting appropriate constants to 0: `T*c0*epsilon + c3*epsilon**3 + c4*epsilon + c5*epsilon**c6 + c9`. With c6=3: `T*c0*epsilon + (c3+c5)*epsilon**3 + c4*epsilon + c9`. Has T*epsilon not T*epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 48:** Has exp and sin terms. Not polynomial. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 49:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2 + c3*epsilon**3 + c4 + c5*epsilon`
With c1=0, c5=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2 + c3*epsilon**3 + c4` ✓ **MATCH**

**Candidate 50:** Already analyzed. **MATCH**

**Candidate 51:** Has exp terms. **NO MATCH** (exp(T*c1) can't be polynomial)

**Candidate 52:** `T*c0 + c1*epsilon + c2 + c3*epsilon**c4 + c5*exp(T*c6)*|epsilon|**c7`
With c6=0: c5*|epsilon|**c7. With c4=3, c7=3, epsilon≥0: `T*c0 + c1*epsilon + c2 + c3*epsilon**3 + c5*epsilon**3` = `T*c0 + c1*epsilon + c2 + (c3+c5)*epsilon**3`. Set c1=0: `T*c0 + c2 + (c3+c5)*epsilon**3`. Missing T*epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 53-71:** These don't have T*epsilon**3 structure (they have T*c0 linear in T, or (c+epsilon)**4, etc.)

Let me check a few more carefully:

**Candidate 56:** `T*c0 + c1*epsilon + c2*epsilon**c3 + c4 + c5*epsilon**c6`
With c3=3, c6=3: `T*c0 + c1*epsilon + (c2+c5)*epsilon**3 + c4`. Missing T*epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 59:** `T*c0 + c1*epsilon + c2 + c3*epsilon**c4 + c5*(c6+|epsilon|)**c7`
No T*epsilon**3 term possible. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 60:** `T*c0 + c1*epsilon + c2 + c3*epsilon**4 + c4*(c5+|epsilon|)**3`
With c5=0, epsilon≥0: c4*epsilon**3. `T*c0 + c1*epsilon + c2 + c3*epsilon**4 + c4*epsilon**3`. Set c1=0, c3=0: `T*c0 + c2 + c4*epsilon**3`. Missing T*epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 61:** `T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + c2*epsilon + c3 + c4*(c5+|epsilon|)**4`
Has T*epsilon not T*epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 62:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**c2 + c3*epsilon + c4 + c5*(c6+|epsilon|)**4`
With c1=0, c2=3: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c3*epsilon + c4 + c5*(c6+|epsilon|)**4`. The (c6+|epsilon|)**4 with c6=0: c5*epsilon**4. Can't get epsilon**3 standalone and T. Set c5=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c3*epsilon + c4`. Missing T and epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 65:** `c0*epsilon + c1 + c2*(c3+|epsilon|)**4 + c4*exp(T*c5)`
exp(T*c5) is not polynomial in T (unless c5=0, giving constant). No T*epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 68:** `T*c0 + T*c1*(epsilon+1)**c2 + T*c3*epsilon + T*c3 + c4*epsilon + c5 + c6*epsilon**c7`
With c2=3: `T*c1*(epsilon+1)**3` expands to include T*epsilon**3. With c1 as coefficient, expanding: `T*c1*(1+3*epsilon+3*epsilon**2+epsilon**3)`. So T*epsilon**3 coefficient is c1. Other T terms: `T*c0 + T*c1 + T*c3 + 3*T*c1*epsilon + T*c3*epsilon + 3*T*c1*epsilon**2`. Need to cancel T*epsilon and T*epsilon**2: set 3*c1+c3=0 and 3*c1=0 → c1=0, but then no T*epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 69:** `T*c0 + T*c1*(c2+epsilon)**c3 + c4*epsilon + c5 + c6*epsilon**c7`
With c3=3, c2=0: `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon**3 + c4*epsilon + c5 + c6*epsilon**c7`. With c7=3, c4=0: `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon**3 + c5 + (c6)*epsilon**3` = `T*c1*epsilon**3 + T*c0 + c5 + c6*epsilon**3` ✓ **MATCH**

**Candidate 70:** `T*c0 + T*c1*(c2+epsilon)**2 + c3*epsilon + c4 + c5*epsilon**4`
T*(c2+epsilon)**2 gives T*epsilon**2 max. No T*epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 71:** `c0*epsilon + c1 + c2*(c3+|epsilon|)**4 + c4*log(T*c5+1)`
log is not polynomial. No T*epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

Now let me also reconsider candidates with `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3` where we DON'T set c1=0 but instead use other terms to cancel the unwanted T*epsilon and T*epsilon**2 terms.

For GT we need: T*epsilon**3, epsilon**3, T, 1 (and nothing else).

**Candidate 15 revisited:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2 + T*c3 + T*c4*epsilon + c5 + c6*epsilon + c7*epsilon**2`
Expanding: `T*c0*c1**3 + 3*T*c0*c1**2*epsilon + 3*T*c0*c1*epsilon**2 + T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*(c2+c3) + T*c4*epsilon + c5 + c6*epsilon + c7*epsilon**2`
T*epsilon**2: 3*c0*c1 = 0 → c1=0 (since c0≠0). Then back to c1=0 case. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 18 revisited:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2 + T*c3*epsilon + c4*epsilon + c5 + c6*epsilon**2`
T*epsilon**2: 3*c0*c1 = 0 → c1=0. Then `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2 + T*c3*epsilon + c4*epsilon + c5 + c6*epsilon**2`. Need T*c3*epsilon = 0 → c3=0. Then `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2 + c4*epsilon + c5 + c6*epsilon**2`. Missing epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 21 revisited:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2*epsilon + c3*epsilon + c4 + c5*epsilon**2`
T*epsilon**2: 3*c0*c1 = 0 → c1=0. Then `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2*epsilon + c3*epsilon + c4 + c5*epsilon**2`. T*c2*epsilon can't be eliminated without losing something. Set c2=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c3*epsilon + c4 + c5*epsilon**2`. Missing T and epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 30 revisited:** With c1≠0: T*epsilon**2 coeff: 3*c0*c1. No other T*epsilon**2 term. So c1=0. **NO MATCH**

Let me also check candidates where the expansion of (c1+epsilon)**3 with c1≠0 could work if other terms cancel:

**Candidate 13 revisited:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2 + T*c3*epsilon + c4*epsilon + c5*epsilon**3 + c6 + c7*epsilon + c8*epsilon**2`
T*epsilon**2: 3*c0*c1 = 0 → c1=0. Already handled. **MATCH** (confirmed above)

**Candidate 10 revisited:** Already confirmed **MATCH**.

**Candidate 14 revisited with c1≠0:** 
`T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2 + T*c3*(c4+epsilon)**c5 + c6 + c7*epsilon + c8*epsilon**2`
If c5=2: `T*c3*(c4+epsilon)**2 = T*c3*(c4**2 + 2*c4*epsilon + epsilon**2)`
T*epsilon**2: 3*c0*c1 + c3 = 0
T*epsilon: 3*c0*c1**2 + 2*c3*c4 = 0
T*epsilon**3: c0
T: c0*c1**3 + c2 + c3*c4**2

From 3*c0*c1 + c3 = 0: c3 = -3*c0*c1
From 3*c0*c1**2 + 2*(-3*c0*c1)*c4 = 0: 3*c0*c1*(c1 - 2*c4) = 0
If c1≠0: c4 = c1/2

Then non-T terms: c6 + c7*epsilon + c8*epsilon**2. We need epsilon**3 and constant. No epsilon**3 available. **NO MATCH**

Now let me verify my matches more carefully:

**Candidate 3:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T**c2*c3 + T**c2*c4*|epsilon|**c5 + c6*|epsilon|**c5 + c7 + c8*epsilon + c9*epsilon**2`
With c1=0, c2=1, c5=3, c8=0, c9=0, epsilon≥0:
`T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c3 + T*c4*epsilon**3 + c6*epsilon**3 + c7`
= `T*(c0+c4)*epsilon**3 + T*c3 + c6*epsilon**3 + c7`
This matches GT form: T*epsilon**3 + T + epsilon**3 + 1 ✓ **MATCH**

**Candidate 5:** With c7=0 (so exp(0)=1), c8=3, c1=0, c4=0, c5=0, epsilon≥0:
`T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2 + c3 + c6*epsilon**3` ✓ **MATCH**

**Candidate 8:** With c1=0, c8=3, c5=0, c6=0, epsilon≥0:
`T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*(c2+c3) + c4 + c7*epsilon**3` ✓ **MATCH**

**Candidate 10:** With c1=0, c4=3, c6=0, c7=0:
`T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2 + c3*epsilon**3 + c5` ✓ **MATCH**

**Candidate 13:** With c1=0, c3=0, c4=0, c7=0, c8=0:
`T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2 + c5*epsilon**3 + c6` ✓ **MATCH**

**Candidate 49:** With c1=0, c5=0:
`T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2 + c3*epsilon**3 + c4` ✓ **MATCH**

**Candidate 50:** With c1=0, c5=0, c6=0:

**Candidate 69:** With c2=0, c3=3, c4=0, c7=3:
`T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon**3 + c5 + c6*epsilon**3` ✓ **MATCH**
